Rp[1])*sum_exp*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent))) + sum_exp*(-0.5*c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*c->exponent*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(sum_exp*sum_exp)*(-Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.25*(sum_exp*sum_exp)*(-Boys[1]*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent))) + 16.0*sum_exp*(c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[2]*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent)) - (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent))))/(p*(sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp)) ;
	val *= d_cgto_normalization_factors[a->basis_index] * d_cgto_normalization_factors[b->basis_index] * d_auxiliary_cgto_normalization_factors[c->basis_index];
	atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(a->basis_index+5) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+1], val * d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+5)]);
	if(is_prim_id_neq) atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(b->basis_index+5) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+1], val * d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index+5)]);
}

// [dyz dyz | pz]
if ( !((g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+5)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold) && (!is_prim_id_neq || g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index+5)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold))) {
	val = coefAndNorm * 0.0625*(4.0*p*(a->coordinate.y - b->coordinate.y)*sum_exp*(-2.0*(a->coordinate.z - b->coordinate.z)*sum_exp*(2.0*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(-Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2]))) + sum_exp*(Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1]))) - 4.0*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(-c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Boys[3]*c->exponent)) - (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(-c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent))) + 4.0*sum_exp*(-c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])))) + 8.0*(a->coordinate.z - b->coordinate.z)*sum_exp*(2.0*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.y + Rp[1])*(Boys[3]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[4]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2])) - (-a->coordinate.y + Rp[1])*sum_exp*(Boys[2]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2]))) - p*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.y + Rp[1])*(Boys[2]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2])) - (-a->coordinate.y + Rp[1])*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2]))) + 0.5*sum_exp*(-Boys[1]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*(sum_exp*sum_exp) + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp + c->exponent*(Boys[2]*(-a->coordinate.z + Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(-c->coordinate.z + Rp[2])))) + sum_exp*(-c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])) + p*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent))) + 16.0*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[2]*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent))) + p*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[2]*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent)) - (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) - p*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[1]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[2]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*sum_exp*(Boys[1]*sum_exp - Boys[2]*c->exponent))) + sum_exp*(-0.5*c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(-Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + 0.5*c->exponent*(c->exponent*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + c->exponent*(Boys[2]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])))))/(p*(sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp)) ;
	val *= d_cgto_normalization_factors[a->basis_index] * d_cgto_normalization_factors[b->basis_index] * d_auxiliary_cgto_normalization_factors[c->basis_index];
	atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(a->basis_index+5) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+2], val * d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+5)]);
	if(is_prim_id_neq) atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(b->basis_index+5) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+2], val * d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index+5)]);
}
